# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="413f5-102">Tipos obsoletos en .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-103">En las tablas de este artículo se muestran los tipos que están obsoletos en [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] y [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] organizados por ensamblados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-104">Utilice los vínculos siguientes para ver una lista de tipos obsoletos y las alternativas recomendadas en cada ensamblado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-105">Dado que estos tipos están en desuso, todos sus miembros también lo están.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-106">Para obtener una lista de miembros obsoletos adicionales de la biblioteca de clases de .NET Framework, vea [Miembros obsoletos](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="413f5-133">Tipos obsoletos en ensamblados del sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-133">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="413f5-134">En las tablas siguientes se enumeran los tipos que se han declarado obsoletos en ensamblados del sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-135">Estos ensamblados se usan para el desarrollo de aplicaciones de uso\-general cuyo destino es .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>   
## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="413f5-925">Tipos obsoletos en ensamblados de Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-925">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="413f5-926">En las secciones siguientes se enumeran los tipos obsoletos en ensamblados de Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-926">The following sections list the obsolete types in Microsoft assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="413f5-927">Estos ensamblados son ensamblados para fines especiales, como ensamblados que están destinados a un lenguaje individual (por ejemplo, Microsoft.JScript.dll o Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-927">These assemblies are special-purpose assemblies such as assemblies that target an individual language (for example, Microsoft.JScript.dll or Microsoft.VisualC.dll).</span></span>  
  
<a name="IEHost"></a>   
### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="413f5-928">Ensamblado: IEHost.dll e IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="413f5-928">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>
